         <script type="text/javascript">
          /* jshint -W100 */
$(document).ready(function() {
	var search = { 
		listPane: null,
		inputForm: null,
		closeBttn: null,
		lastCall: null,
		selectSite: 0,
		init: function() {
			var prevText = '';
			this.inputForm = $('div.h_searchBar').find('input[type="search"]');
			this.listPane = $('div.h_searchBar').find('div.search_result');
			this.closeBttn = $('div.h_searchBar').find('div.command > a.close');
			this.lastCall = new Date();
			this.inputForm.on({
				keyup: function(e) {
					//검색 
					var str = $.trim($(this).val());
					if (prevText != str) {
						prevText = str;
						if (str.length) {
							search.doSearch(str, ['site']);
						} else {
							search.listPane.removeClass('list show').find('ul').html('');//초기화  
						}
						this.selectSite = 0; 
						$('.search_result ul').scrollTop(0);
					}
 					
 					// ↑: 38 ↓ : 40
					if(e.keyCode == 40 || e.keyCode == 38){
						searchResult = $('div.search_result').find('ul > li');  
						searchCount = searchResult.length;
						searchResult.removeClass('active');
						if(e.keyCode == 40){ 
							if(searchCount > this.selectSite){
								searchResult.eq(this.selectSite).addClass('active');
								this.selectSite++;  
							}else if(searchCount == this.selectSite){
								searchResult.eq(this.selectSite-1).addClass('active');
							}
						}else{
							if(this.selectSite == 0 || this.selectSite == 1){
								if(this.selectSite){
									searchResult.eq(0).addClass('active');
								}
							 	
							 	scrollpx = 0;  
							}else{
								this.selectSite--;
								searchResult.eq(this.selectSite-1).addClass('active'); 
							}
						}  

						//console.log('t:'+searchCount+'//c:'+this.selectSite); 

						 scrollpx = Math.floor(this.selectSite)*30; 
						 if(scrollpx > 0){
						 	$('.search_result ul').scrollTop(scrollpx-90); 
						 }
					}else if(e.keyCode == 13){// enter 
						if(this.selectSite > 0){
							//onsole.log(searchResult.eq(this.selectSite-1).find('a').attr('href'));
							location.href = searchResult.eq(this.selectSite-1).find('a').attr('href');
						}
					}else{	//초기화 
						this.selectSite = 0; 
						$('.search_result ul').scrollTop(0);
					}
 
 
				},
				focus: function() { 
					prevText = '';
					//$(this).keyup(); 
				},
				blur: function() {  
					//console.log(search.listPane.find('*:focus')); 

// /					console.log($(this).val());
					//  if (!search.listPane.find('a:focus').length && !jQuery.browser.msie) {
					// 	search.listPane.removeClass('list show nolist');
					// 	//초기화 
					// 	this.selectSite = 0; 
					// 	$('.search_result ul').scrollTop(0);
					// }

					//익스 예외처리 
					// if(jQuery.browser.msie){ 
						if(search.listPane.hasClass('nolist')){
							search.listPane.removeClass('list show nolist');
							//초기화 
							this.selectSite = 0; 
							$('.search_result ul').scrollTop(0);
						}
					//}
				} 
			});
			this.listPane.on('mousedown mouseup click', 'a', function(e) { 
				//console.log(e);
				search.inputForm.focus();
				if (e.type != 'click') {
					e.preventDefault();
				}

			});
			this.closeBttn.on('click', function(e) { 
				search.listPane.removeClass('show');
				e.preventDefault();
			});
			var searchWord = '';
			$('#h_searchBar_form').submit(function(e) {
				//$(this).find('input').prop('disabled', 'disabled');
				// search.inputForm.blur();
				// if (search.inputForm.val() == searchWord) { e.preventDefault(); return false; }
				// else { searchWord = search.inputForm.val(); }
				return false;
			});
		},
		doSearch: function(str, option) {
			this.lastCall = new Date();
			$.ajax({
				type: 'POST', 
				url: 'http://www.inven.co.kr/common/quicklink/search.ajax.php',
				dataType: 'json',
				data: { search: str, target: option, searchID: this.lastCall, maxLength: 20 }
			}).success(this.onSuccess).fail(this.onFail);
		},
		onSuccess: function(r) {
			var part, list, i, txt, data = r.data, ul, nolist = true;
			ul = search.listPane.removeClass('list show').find('ul');
			ul.html('');
			if (r) {
				if (r.data && r.searchID) {
					if (r.searchID != search.lastCall) { return 0; }
					for (part in data) {
						if (!data.hasOwnProperty(part)) { continue; }
						list = data[part];
						if (list.length || typeof list.constructor == 'function') {
							for (i in list) {
								if (list.hasOwnProperty(i)) {
									if (nolist) { nolist = false; }
									txt = list[i]; 
									if (part == 'site') {
										txt.link = txt.link.replace("http://m.inven.co.kr/",""); 
										if(txt.link.indexOf('?site=') == 0){  
											txt.link = txt.link.replace(/\//g,""); 
											txt.link = txt.link.replace("?site=","");  
											txt.link = "http://game.inven.co.kr/"+txt.link;
										}else{
											txt.link = txt.link.replace("?site=","");  
											txt.link = txt.link.replace(/\//g,""); 
											txt.link = "http://"+txt.link+".inven.co.kr"; 
										}
										//console.log(txt.link);
										ul.append('<li class="site site-' + i + '"><a href="' + txt.link + '" title=""><img src="http://static.inven.co.kr/image_2011/common/channel/icon_32x32_' + txt.icon + '.gif?v=160615a" alt="' + txt.name + '">' + txt.name + '</a></li>');
									}
								}
							}
							if (nolist) {
								search.listPane.removeClass('list').addClass('show nolist').find('p').text('추천 검색어가 없습니다.');
							}
							ul.scrollTop(0);
						} else {
							search.listPane.removeClass('list').addClass('show nolist').find('p').text('추천 검색어가 없습니다.');
						}
					}
					if (ul.find('> li').length) {
						search.listPane.removeClass('nolist').addClass('show list');
					}
					return 1;
				} else {
					search.listPane.removeClass('list').addClass('show nolist').find('p').text('검색오류가 발생하였습니다.');
				}
			} else {
				search.listPane.removeClass('list').addClass('show nolist').find('p').text('검색오류가 발생하였습니다.');
			}
			return 0;
		},
		onFail: function() {
			search.listPane.removeClass('list').addClass('show nolist').find('p').text('검색오류가 발생하였습니다.');
		}
	};
	search.init(); 
			
		$("#comHeadQuickLink .quickMain button").click(function(e){ 


			if(this.hasAttribute('quick-search-code')){   // 초성 검색 버튼 
				$("#kanada button").removeClass('active');    
				$(this).addClass('active');
				$('#kanada div').addClass('hidden'); 
				$('#kanada .topMenu').removeClass('hidden');
				$('#kanada div.'+this.getAttribute('quick-search-code')).removeClass('hidden');

			}else{ //  장르별/가나다순 
				$("#comHeadQuickLink button").removeClass('active');    
				$(this).addClass('active');
			}

			if($(this).hasClass('genre')){	// 장르별 
				$('.genre').removeClass('hidden'); 
				$('#kanada').addClass('hidden');
			}

			if($(this).hasClass('kanada')){	// 가나다 
				$('#genre').addClass('hidden'); 
				$('#kanada').removeClass('hidden');
				$('#kanada div').addClass('hidden'); 
				$('#kanada .topMenu').removeClass('hidden');
				$('#kanada .topMenu button.tab1').addClass('active');
				$('#kanada .all').removeClass('hidden');
			}


		}); 

		// 퀵링크 닫기 
	    $("#comHeadQuickLink .backdrop").click(function (e) {
	        var target = e.target; 
	        if ($(target).hasClass("backdrop")) {
	        	INVEN.quickLink.openQuickLinkNew(this, 'w-0', 's+0'); 
	        	$('div.h_searchBar').find('input[type="search"]').val('');
	        }
	    });
	    $("#comHeadQuickLink .quicklink_close").click(function (e) { 
        	INVEN.quickLink.openQuickLinkNew(this, 'w-0', 's+0'); 
        	$('div.h_searchBar').find('input[type="search"]').val('');
	    });

	    $("input[name=search]").keydown(function(key){
	    	if(key.keyCode == 13){	//엔터실행 불가 
	    		return false;
	    	}
	    });
 
	});
         </script>

     <div id="webzineTop">
      <div class="mainLogo " id="mainLogo">
       <a href="http://www.inven.co.kr/webzine">
        인벤
       </a>

       <script type="text/javascript">
        INVEN.Ad.showTopRight2('webzine');
       </script>
      </div>
     </div>
     <script type="text/javascript">
      var WEBZINE = window.WEBZINE || {};
	WEBZINE.Layout = WEBZINE.Layout || {};
	WEBZINE.Layout.headmenu  = function() {
		var pObj;
		var mObj;
		var sObj;
		var delay;
		var overObj;
		var fixMenu;
		var criteria = new Array();
		criteria['showdelay'] = 0;
		criteria['hidedelay'] = 500;
		criteria['subindent'] = 10;
		var thisObj = this;
		this.init = function(obj, subObj) {
			obj = getObj(obj);
			mObj = obj;
			pObj = mObj.parentNode;
			sObj = getObj(subObj);
			if (criteria['type'] == 'layer') {
				sObj.style.position = 'absolute';
			}
			if (criteria['type'] == 'fixlayout') {
				sObj.style.display = 'inline';
				sObj = INVEN.Html.getChildNodes(sObj, 'div', true)[0];
				sObj.style.display = 'none';
			}
			memuAction();
		}
		this.setFixMenu = function(value) {
			this.fixMenu = value;
		}
		this.setACriteria = function(option, value) {
			criteria[option] = value;
		}
		function inArray(array, value) {
			for (var i = 0; i < array.length; i++) {
				if (array[i] == value) {
					return true;
				}
			}
			return false;
		}
		function memuAction() {
			var overObjArray = new Array();
			var ulObjs = INVEN.Html.getChildNodes(sObj, 'ul');
			var tempObj = INVEN.Html.getChildNodes(mObj, 'ul', true)[0];
			var liObjs = INVEN.Html.getChildNodes(tempObj, 'li', true);
			for (var i = 0; i < liObjs.length; i++) {
				var liObj = liObjs[i];
				var subMenuObj = INVEN.Html.getChildNodes(liObj, 'ul', true)[0];
				if (subMenuObj) {
					var tempSubMenuObj = sObj;
					if (criteria['type'] == 'fixlayout') {
						liObj.removeChild(subMenuObj);
					} else {
						tempSubMenuObj = INVEN.Html.getChildNodes(tempSubMenuObj, 'div', true)[0];
						liObj.removeChild(subMenuObj);
					}
					tempSubMenuObj.appendChild(subMenuObj);
					overObjArray.push(subMenuObj.className);
				}
				if (!thisObj.fixMenu) {
					if (inArray(overObjArray, liObj.className)) {
						liObj.onmouseover = function() {
							menuOverFn(this);
						}
						liObj.onmouseout = function() {
							menuOutFn();
						}
					}
				}
			}
			for (var i = 0; i < overObjArray.length; i++) {
				if (overObjArray[i] == thisObj.fixMenu) {
					menuOverFn(liObjs[i]);
				}
			}
			if (!thisObj.fixMenu) {
				sObj.onmouseover = function() {
					menuOverFn();
				}
				sObj.onmouseout = function() {
					menuOutFn();
				}
			}
		}
		function menuOverFn(over) {
			clearTimeout(delay);
			overObj = over;
			delay = setTimeout(menuOver, criteria['showdelay']);
		}
		function menuOutFn() {
			clearTimeout(delay);
			delay = setTimeout(menuOut, criteria['hidedelay']);
		}
		function menuOver() {
			if (overObj) {
				var overObjParentPos = INVEN.Coordination.getAbsPos(overObj.parentNode);
				var overObjPos = INVEN.Coordination.getAbsPos(overObj);
				var overObjPosResX = overObjPos.x - overObjParentPos.x;
				var ulObjs = INVEN.Html.getChildNodes(sObj, 'ul');
				var fixPosition = 0;
				for (var i = 0; i < ulObjs.length; i++) {
					var ulObj = ulObjs[i];
					ulObj.style.display = 'none';
					if (overObj.className == ulObj.className) {
						fixPosition = overObjPosResX + criteria['subindent'];
						ulObj.style.display = 'inline';
						var totalWidth = 0;
						var menuWidth = 0;
						var liObjs = INVEN.Html.getChildNodes(ulObj, 'li', true);
						sObj.style.display = 'inline';
						for (j = 0; j < liObjs.length; j++) {
							var liObj = liObjs[j];
							totalWidth += liObj.offsetWidth;
						}
						menuWidth = sObj.offsetWidth;
						/* Opera에서 오른쪽 넘어가는 서브메뉴 위치 재계산시 문제 발생 (layoutfix 일때) */
						/* 넓이를 상위 메뉴 크기로 고정 */
							menuWidth = mObj.offsetWidth;
						sObj.style.display = 'none';
						if (totalWidth + fixPosition > menuWidth) {
							fixPosition = menuWidth - totalWidth;
						}
					}
				}
				ulObj.parentNode.style.marginLeft = fixPosition + 'px';
			}
			if ((criteria['type'] == 'layer') && (sObj.parentNode.nodeName.toLowerCase() != 'body') && document.body) {
				if (!INVEN.Layer.ready) return;
				INVEN.Layer.show(sObj, 'wf+0', 'n+29', '', true, pObj);
			}
			sObj.style.display = 'inline';
		}
		function menuOut() {
			if (criteria['type'] == 'layer') {
				INVEN.Layer.hide(sObj);
			}
			sObj.style.display = 'none';
		}
	}
     </script>

     <script type="text/javascript">
      var webzineHeadmenuObject = new WEBZINE.Layout.headmenu();
	//webzineHeadmenuObject.setACriteria('showdelay', 0);
	//webzineHeadmenuObject.setACriteria('hidedelay', 500);
	//webzineHeadmenuObject.setACriteria('subindent', 10);
	//webzineHeadmenuObject.setACriteria('type', 'layer');
	webzineHeadmenuObject.setACriteria('type', 'fixlayout');
	webzineHeadmenuObject.setFixMenu('news');
	webzineHeadmenuObject.init('webzineHeadmenuMain', 'webzineHeadmenuSub');

     <script type="text/javascript">
      //var webzineHeadmenuForm1 = INVEN.Html.FormControl.create();
	//webzineHeadmenuForm1.setForm('webzineHeadmenuF1');
	//webzineHeadmenuForm1.addField('sw','검색어');
	//webzineHeadmenuForm1.getForm().onsubmit = function() { isearch_community(); }

    $("#webzineHeadmenuF1 input[name='sw']").keydown(function(key){
    	if(key.keyCode == 13){	//엔터실행   
			isearch_community();
    		return false;
    	}
    });

    $('#webzineHeadmenuF1 .submit').click(function(e){
		isearch_community();
        return false;
    });

	// 검색 
	function isearch_community(){
		url = 'http://www.inven.co.kr/search';
		skin = 'webzine';
		page = 1;
		type = 'top';
		isearchword = $('#webzineHeadmenuF1 input[name=sw]').val();
 
		isearchword = isearchword.replace(/\\/g, "");
		isearchword = isearchword.replace(/\"/g, "");
		isearchword = isearchword.replace(/\'/g, "");
		isearchword = isearchword.replace(/\`/g, "");
		//isearchword = isearchword.replace(/ /gi, ''); 
 
		if(!isearchword){
			url = url + '/' + skin + '/' + type + '/'; 
		}else{
			isearchword = encodeURIComponent(isearchword);
			url = url + '/' + skin + '/' + type + '/' + isearchword + '/' + page;
		}
	  
		document.location.href=url;
		return false;
	}
     </script>

           <script>
            /* SlideHotissue */
		WEBZINE.Home.SlideHotissue = window.WEBZINE.Home.SlideHotissue || {};
		WEBZINE.Home.SlideHotissue.readyHotissue = function() {
			var totalCount = $(".centerPart ul li").length;
			var widthLimit = ((totalCount - 6) * 103) * -1;
			var listWidth  = totalCount * 103;
			var moveSpeed  = 400;
			var tmpCheck   = true;
			$(".centerPart ul").css('width', listWidth);
			if(totalCount>=7) {
				$(".leftArrowPart a").click(function(e) { if(tmpCheck)  { onMoveHotissue('left');  } e.preventDefault(); });
				$(".rightArrowPart a").click(function(e) { if(tmpCheck) { onMoveHotissue('right'); } e.preventDefault(); });
			} else {
				$(".rightArrowPart a").addClass('lock');
				$(".leftArrowPart a, .rightArrowPart a").click(function(e) { e.preventDefault(); });
			}
			function onMoveHotissue(type) {
				tmpCheck = false;
				var tempNum = parseInt($(".centerPart ul").css("margin-left"));
				if(type=='left') {
					if((tempNum+618) >= 0) {
						$(".centerPart ul").animate({'margin-left': '0px'}, moveSpeed, moveLock);
						if(totalCount >= 7) { $(".rightArrowPart a").removeClass('lock'); }
					} else {
						$(".centerPart ul").animate({'margin-left': '+=618px'}, moveSpeed, moveLock);
						$(".rightArrowPart a").removeClass('lock');
					}
				} else if(type=='right'){
					if((tempNum+(-618)) <= widthLimit) {
						$(".centerPart ul").animate({"margin-left" : widthLimit}, moveSpeed, moveLock);
						if(totalCount >= 7) { $(".leftArrowPart a").removeClass('lock'); }
					} else {
						$(".centerPart ul").animate({"margin-left" : "-=618px"}, moveSpeed, moveLock);
						$(".leftArrowPart a").removeClass('lock');
					}
				}
			}
			function moveLock() {
				var tempNum = parseInt($(".centerPart ul").css("margin-left"));
				if(tempNum == 0) {$(".leftArrowPart a").addClass('lock');}
				if(tempNum == widthLimit) {$(".rightArrowPart a").addClass('lock');}
				tmpCheck = true;
			}
		}

		WEBZINE.Home.SlideHotissue.mainImageCt = function(tgNum) {
			$(".hotissueImage li a").css('display', 'none');
			$(".hotissueImage li:eq("+tgNum+") a").fadeTo(300,1.0); 
			$(".centerPart ul li a").removeClass('selected');
			$(".centerPart ul li:eq("+tgNum+") a").addClass('selected');
		}
		//임시1
		WEBZINE.Home.SlideHotissue.mainImageCt2 = function(tgNum, mainImage, tmpSrc) {
			var tmpHtml = '';
			tmpHtml += '<a href="'+tmpSrc+'" onfocus="blur();"><img src="'+mainImage+'" /></a>';
			$(".hotissueImage").html(tmpHtml);
			$(".centerPart ul li a").removeClass('selected');
			$(".centerPart ul li:eq("+tgNum+") a").addClass('selected');
			
		}
		//임시2
		WEBZINE.Home.SlideHotissue.mainImageCt3 = function(tgNum) {
			$(".hotissueImage li img").css('display', 'none');
			$(".hotissueImage li:eq("+tgNum+") img").css('display', 'block');
			$(".centerPart ul li a").removeClass('selected');
			$(".centerPart ul li:eq("+tgNum+") a").addClass('selected');
		}
	$(document).ready(function() {
		/* Slide hot issue */
		var tmpRandom = Math.floor(Math.random() * 6);
		WEBZINE.Home.SlideHotissue.mainImageCt(tmpRandom); 
		WEBZINE.Home.SlideHotissue.readyHotissue();
	});
           </script>

              <script type="text/javascript">
               $(document).ready(function() {
        var E3Wrap = $('#e3event');
        E3Wrap.find('.wrap342GR3 .photoList .btn.e3').on('click', function(e) {
            var me = $(this);
            var ul = me.siblings('ul.e3photo');
            var width = ul.width();
                left = Math.abs(parseInt(ul.css('margin-left')));
                move = 341;
            if (me.hasClass('btnRight')) {
                if (ul.is(':not(.animate)')) {
                    ul.addClass('animate').animate({ marginLeft: ((left + move < width) ? ('-=' + move) : '0') + 'px' }, { duration: 500, complete: function() { ul.removeClass('animate'); } });
                }
            } else {
                if (ul.is(':not(.animate)')) {
                    ul.addClass('animate').animate({ marginLeft: ((left - move >= 0) ? ('+=' + move) : ('-=' + Math.floor((width - 1) / move) * move)) + 'px' }, { duration: 500, complete: function() { ul.removeClass('animate'); } });
                }
            }
            e.preventDefault();
        });
    });
              </script>

              <script type="text/javascript">
               var WEBZINE = window.WEBZINE || {};
                WEBZINE.Home = window.WEBZINE.Home || {};
                WEBZINE.Home.newsTabChange = function(obj, wrapObj, tab) {
                    obj = getObj(obj);
                    var tabsObj = getObj(wrapObj + 'Tabs');
                    wrapObj = getObj(wrapObj);
                    var tabObjs = INVEN.Html.getChildNodes(tabsObj, 'a');
                    switch (tab) {
                        case '1':
                            wrapObj.className = 'tabGroup tabGroup1 wrap342AQ1';
                            tabObjs[0].className = 'tab122AQ1 tab122AQ1-CommentTop tab122AQ1-CommentTop-Selected';
                            tabObjs[1].className = 'tab122AQ1 tab122AQ1-ReadTop';
                            break;
                        case '2':
                            wrapObj.className = 'tabGroup tabGroup2 wrap342AQ1';
                            tabObjs[0].className = 'tab122AQ1 tab122AQ1-CommentTop';
                            tabObjs[1].className = 'tab122AQ1 tab122AQ1-ReadTop tab122AQ1-ReadTop-Selected';
                            break;
                    }
                    obj.blur();
                }
              </script>

            <script>
             $("#webzine_20180528 .corner.btn_tab .btn.tab").on("mouseover", function() {
		showBottomCornerTab( $(this) );
	});	

	function showBottomCornerTab(tarObj,randnum){
		var btn = $("#webzine_20180528 .btn_tab .btn");
		var wrap = $("#webzine_20180528 .corner_wrap");
		var cornerIdx = false;
		if(randnum){  cornerIdx = randnum; }
		else{	cornerIdx = tarObj.index();	}
		cornerIdx++;
		btn.removeClass('active');
		if(randnum){
			btn.eq(randnum).addClass('active');	
		}else{
			tarObj.addClass('active');	
		}
		wrap.removeClass('active');
		wrap.filter('[data-corner="'+ cornerIdx +'"]').addClass('active');	
	}

	
	var ranNum = Math.floor(Math.random()*4);
	showBottomCornerTab(false,ranNum);
            </script>

           <script>
            var game_list_check = 'N';
		var game_list_check_yn = 'N';
		var game_list_open_close = 'N';

		function game_pc_list_open(){
			$('#game_more').html('더보기 ▲');
			$('#game_list_mask').removeClass('hide');
			$('.sub-game-list').fadeIn();
			game_list_check = 'Y';
            game_list_open_close = 'Y';
		}
		function game_pc_list_close(){
			$('#game_more').html('더보기 ▼');
			$('#game_list_mask').addClass('hide');
			$('.sub-game-list').fadeOut('fast');
			game_list_check = 'N';
            game_list_open_close = 'N';
		}
		
		$("#game_more").on('mouseover', function (){
			if(game_list_check == 'N'){
				game_pc_list_open();
			}
		});
		$("#game_list_mask").on('click', function() {
			game_pc_list_close();
		});
		
		$("#main-game-list > .custom_game_pc_button").on('mouseover', function () {
			if(game_list_check == 'Y' || game_list_check_yn == 'Y'){
				return;
			}
			var num = $(this).data( "custom_game_pc_num" );
			$('.custom_game_pc_button').removeClass('active');
			$('.custom_game_pc_button_'+num).addClass('active');
			$('.custom_game_pc_item_group').addClass('hide');
			$('.custom_game_pc_item_group_'+num).removeClass('hide');
			
			if(game_list_check_yn == 'Y'){
				game_pc_list_close();
			}
		});

        $(".custom-game-pc").mouseleave(function () {
            game_pc_list_close();
        });

		$(".custom_game_pc_button").on('click', function() {
			var num = $(this).data( "custom_game_pc_num" );
			$('.custom_game_pc_button').removeClass('active');
			$('.custom_game_pc_button_'+num).addClass('active');
			$('.custom_game_pc_item_group').addClass('hide');
			$('.custom_game_pc_item_group_'+num).removeClass('hide');
			
			if(game_list_check == 'Y'){
				game_pc_list_close();
			}
			game_list_check_yn = 'Y';
		});
           </script>

           <script type="text/javascript">
            $(document).ready(function () {
    $('#brandpageTabs ul li a').mouseover(function () {
        var selectTab =$(this).attr('data-tab');

        $('#brandpageTabs ul li a').removeClass('tabMenu-Selected');
        $(this).addClass('tabMenu-Selected');

        $('#brandpageList div.tabContent').hide();
        $('#Brand'+selectTab).show();
    });
    $('#Brandtab9').show();
});
           </script>

           <script type="text/javascript">
            var totalCount = $(".articleBody ul li").length;
	var modwidth = 202-2;
	var listWidth  = totalCount * modwidth;
	var widthLimit = ((totalCount - 1) * modwidth) * -1;
	var moveSpeed  = 500;
	var tmpCheck   = true;

	$(".articleBody ul").css('width', listWidth);
	$(".leftArrow a").click(function() { onMoveHotissue('left'); });
	$(".rightArrow a").click(function() { onMoveHotissue('right'); });


	function onMoveHotissue(type) {
		tmpCheck = false;
		var tempNum = parseInt($(".articleBody ul").css("margin-left"));
		if(type=="left"){
			if((tempNum+modwidth) > 0) {
				$(".articleBody ul").animate({"margin-left" : widthLimit}, 200);
			}else{
				$(".articleBody ul").animate({"margin-left" : "+="+(modwidth)+"px"}, moveSpeed);
			}
		}else{
			if((tempNum-modwidth) < widthLimit) {
				$(".articleBody ul").animate({"margin-left" : "0px"}, 200);
			}else{
				$(".articleBody ul").animate({"margin-left" : "-="+(modwidth)+"px"}, moveSpeed);
			}
		}
	}
           </script>

           <script type="text/javascript">
            function onWeekOver(tgNum) {
	$(".broadSchedule .contents ul li").css('display', 'none');
	$(".broadSchedule .contents ul li.week"+tgNum).css('display', 'block');
}
$(document).ready(function() {
	onWeekOver(5); 
	$(".broadSchedule .week ul li a").mouseout(function() {
		onWeekOver(5); 
	});
});
           </script>
